<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скотч.html>скотч</a> (22890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Scotch tape</i>, but the meaning has expanded beyond the corresponding meaning in English.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скотч.html>скотч</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skotč</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скотч.html>ско́тча</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скотч.html>ско́тчи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скотч.html>ско́тчей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>adhesive tape</li></ol>

***скрёбшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрёбшийся.html>скрёбшийся</a> (20789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***скрашивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрашивать.html>скра́шивать</a> (29092)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">скра́сить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrásitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрашивать.html>скра́шивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrášivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">скра́сить</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soften, to mitigate (something painful)</li>
<li>to brighten, to make more attractive (something dull or boring)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***скрепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a> (17454)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепить.html>крепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fasten <i>(together)</i>, to pin <i>(together)</i>, to tie, to clamp, to bolt, to mortar</li>
<li>to strengthen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>скрепя́</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepjá</b> sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reluctantly; grudgingly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seal, to sign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́тью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepítʹ</b> dokumént pečátʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attach a seal to the document</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepítʹ</b> pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sign; fix one's signature</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepítʹ</b> vtorój pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to countersign</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплённый.html>скреплённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljónnyj</b> króvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sealed with blood (friendship etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***скрепка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрепка.html>скре́пка</a> (26044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепка.html>скре́пка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrépka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепка.html>скре́пки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепка.html>скре́пки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепка.html>скре́пок</a></b>)
</p>

***скреплять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a> (25919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrepljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрепить.html>скрепи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fasten <i>(together)</i>, to pin <i>(together)</i>, to tie, to clamp, to bolt, to mortar</li>
<li>to strengthen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>скрепя́</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepjá</b> sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reluctantly; grudgingly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to seal, to sign
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:документ.html>докуме́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печать.html>печа́тью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljátʹ</b> dokumént pečátʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to attach a seal to the document</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljátʹ</b> pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sign; fix one's signature</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплять.html>скрепля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подпись.html>по́дписью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljátʹ</b> vtorój pódpisʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to countersign</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скреплённый.html>скреплённый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кро́вью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrepljónnyj</b> króvʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sealed with blood (friendship etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">скре́па</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skrépa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krépkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепкий.html>кре́пко</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krépko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепление.html>крепле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kreplénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***скрести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́</a> (12899)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skresti</i>, cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">скребти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrebtý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">скрэ́бці</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrébci</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***скрестить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́ть</a> (8007)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крестить.html>крести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрещивать.html>скре́щивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cross
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грудь.html>груди</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrestítʹ</b> ruki na grudi</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to fold one's arms</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>skrestítʹ</b> nogi</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to cross one's legs</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шпага.html>шпа́ги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skrestítʹ špági</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross swords</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрестить.html>скрести́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оружие.html>ору́жие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skrestítʹ orúžije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cross weapon</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cross, to crossbreed</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скривиться.html>скриви́ться</a> (13198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скривить.html>скриви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скривиться.html>скриви́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrivítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривиться.html>криви́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become crooked/bent/lopsided</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a face</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скривить.html>скриви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skrivítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***скрипевший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́вший</a> (4238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skripévšij</span>)
</p>

***скрипеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́ть</a> (4238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skripétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскрипеть.html>проскрипе́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипнуть.html>скри́пнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to creak, to screech, to squeak <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a prolonged sharp grating or squeaking sound</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипи́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:потертый.html>потёртое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:седло.html>седло́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Opjátʹ <b>skripít</b> potjórtoje sedló</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The worn out saddle is creaking again.</span></dd><dl><dd>(<span class="e-source">from a song</span>)</dd></dl></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрипка.html>скри́пка</a> (5579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skripétʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to creak</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. </p>

***скрипнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрипнуть.html>скри́пнуть</a> (7034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипнуть.html>скри́пнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skrípnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to creak, to screech, to squeak <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make a prolonged sharp grating or squeaking sound</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдруг.html>Вдруг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зке</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипнуть.html>скри́пнула</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a> (from a song).</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vdrug kak v skázke <b>skrípnula</b> dverʹ (from a song).</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Suddenly, like in a fairy tale, the door squeaked.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***скрипучий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скрипучий.html>скрипу́чий</a> (7779)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипеть.html>скрипе́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skripétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-účij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скрипучий.html>скрипу́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skripúčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>creaky, squeaky</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> harsh, unpleasant, rasping <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sound, voice, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
